font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿旺益西（藏）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、阿吾勒别克·努尔加合蒲（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿亚桑扎（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">艾朝玉、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">艾则孜•艾买提（维）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安然、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安彦魁</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、昂扎（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">奥坎（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">阿布都热扎克·沙依木</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">1957</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月出生，新疆维吾尔自治区阿克苏地区柯坪县人，维吾尔族名：</span><span style="font-family: &quot;MS Gothic&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Gothic&quot;;">‎</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">Abdurazaq Sayim ئابدۇرازاق سايىم</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">，新疆乌鲁木齐市新城区北京路街道中英公小区居民，中共党员，公职人员，早期曾为新疆自治区教育厅工农教育处、自治区成人招生办和自治区招生办干事，后任自治区招生办副主任、新疆教育报刊社副总编、阿克苏地区温宿县委副书记、自治区教委勤工俭学办主任，原新疆教育出版社党委副书记、社长、副总编，原新疆社会科学院党委委员、副院长，以沙塔尔·沙吾提为首的分裂国家犯罪集团的要犯之一，中共新疆当局指称的“双面人”，中国在押政治犯。自</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2016</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年以来，因中共新疆当局对维吾尔族等各少数族裔实行更严格的高压管控，其虽长期就职于当局任命的高级公职岗位上，但依然为中共新疆当局视为可猜疑得异己，暗中监控，收集欲打压资料；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2016</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">29</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">日，其被新疆维吾尔自治区纪委突然以涉嫌严重违纪为由停职工作，接受组织调查；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">25</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">日，经新疆自治区党委批准，准予自治区纪委对其严重违纪问题进行立案审查；后其被很快开除党籍、开除公职（即“双开”）和收缴违纪所得，且自治区纪委将其涉嫌犯罪问题及线索移送至新疆维吾尔自治区检察院处置；同年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">日，其案被自治区检察院以涉嫌“受贿罪”立案侦查，并采取强制措施，指控其因十数年“严重违反政治纪律；严重违反廉洁纪律，收受礼金”和“严重违反国家法律法规，利用职权或者地位形成的便利条件，通过直接安排或向他人打招呼的方式，在企业经营、承揽工程等方面为他人谋取利益，索要、收受巨额财物”，故而涉嫌犯罪，应予批捕；后被又追加罪责，认定其为“以沙塔尔·沙吾提为首的分裂国家犯罪集团”的要犯之一，提起公诉；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12.0pt;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月，其一行多人案在新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐市法院开庭审理，最终其被以“受贿罪”、“分裂国家政权罪”等多项罪名判处无期徒刑；其等不服判决，立即上诉，最高法院已驳回上诉，维持原判；截至目前，一直无法获取其具体信息。目前服刑地址不明。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">阿布杜热扎克•夏木西丁（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊宁市人，伊宁市克拜克玉孜村农民，曾当过木工，维吾尔名<span lang="EN-US">Abdurazzak Shamseden</span>，新疆著名持不同政见者。<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年曾因其胞弟萨迪尔丁·夏木西丁<span lang="EN-US">(Sadirdin Shamseden)</span>发起一个旨在解决维吾尔人酗酒及毒品泛滥等社会问题的民间草根运动（又叫“麦西莱普活动”），其亦参与其中。尽管几年间该运动发展日益壮大，覆盖了几乎整个伊宁周边地区，但终因碰触到中共高层的敏感神经，引起中共新疆当局的极度恐慌，遂遭强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年麦西莱普活动被政府明令禁止；<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日新疆伊宁发生维吾尔族市民大规模抗议游行示威，虽被很快强力镇压，但之后伊宁地区的胡迪亚玉孜村又发生了警民冲突，且又有六人被军警枪杀，因其外甥哈穆提•莫哈买提<span lang="EN-US">(Hemmat Muhemmet)</span>是警民冲突中死亡青年之一，所以其亦被怀疑参与其中。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被当局抓捕，并被指控与<span lang="EN-US">2.5</span>伊宁抗议示威及本次警民冲突有关；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月其被伊宁市中级法院以“分裂国家罪”判处无期徒刑，剥夺政治权利终身；其不服上诉，二审后依然维持原判；据悉其惨遭刑讯逼供和极端非人待遇；审讯和审判期间，几乎所有人道权利及法律基本权利均被剥夺，既无任何法律代理，又不准与家属见面，其家属不仅没有接到审判日通知，判决书中也无确切审判日期，亲属只是在上诉截止日前三天，才由小道消息获此判决信息。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐第一监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿布拉江·阿乌提·阿有普（<span lang="EN-US">Ablajan Awut Ayup</span>）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">维吾尔族、新疆和田人，是极受维吾尔人欢迎的维吾尔青年歌手，因为颂歌维吾尔人而被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被新疆当局重判<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿尔恒•巴杂尔别克（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">阿里木江•依米提（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区哈密市人，原英资企业新疆佳尔豪氏食品有限公司喀什分公司经理，曾信仰伊斯兰教，后改信基督教，喀什地区基督教传道人，中国在押良心犯。曾因在新疆喀什地区举办基督教家庭教会活动，并积极传播基督教义和发展基督教徒等，触碰到了中共当局的意识形态底线，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，被新疆喀什市民族宗教事务局认定为“<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年以来，以工作名义，在喀什地区非法从事宗教渗透活动，在维吾尔族群众中传播基督教，散发宗教宣传品，发展基督教徒”；<span lang="EN-US"> 2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，喀什市警方突然将其带走，随即以“涉嫌煽动分裂国家罪”和 “向境外非法提供国家秘密罪”将其刑事拘留，关押于新疆喀什市看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被当地检察院正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，新疆喀什中级法院对其进行了秘密开庭审理，后因证据不足，被法庭退回当地警方补充侦查；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被喀市地区中级法院再次秘审，被以“向境外人员非法提供国家秘密罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被新疆自治区高级法院重审，最终仍以<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年（ “绝密”级别量刑）维持原判。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区第三监狱服刑；据悉，在关押期间其曾遭酷刑毒打，被送进喀什农三师医院救治；其妻探监亦由每个月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>分钟探视时间减少到每三个月一次仅<span lang="EN-US">10</span>分钟；截止<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因当地警方和社区管理部门不予开具准许探视证明，其妻探监再遭刁难。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿斯哈·阿孜提别克（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，哈萨克族，原伊宁市飞机场路<span lang="EN-US">61</span>号北苑别墅区居民，前伊犁哈萨克自治州察布查尔锡伯自治县粮食局官员，原伊犁哈萨克自治州政府移民管理局退休干部，哈萨克国籍公民，中国在押政治犯。因其曾在伊犁州政府移民管理局工作期间，接触过伊犁河流域水利工程的移民搬迁工作，熟知伊犁河是中哈国际河流和涉伊犁河流域相关水利工程项目，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月又与哈萨克共和国驻中国乌鲁木齐签证代办处副主任达尼亚尔·赛力克巴耶夫<span lang="EN-US">(SERIKBAYEV DANIYAR)</span>相结识，遂遭中共新疆当局的高度警觉、监控与强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，其已移民至哈萨克斯坦国（以下简称“哈国”），并于同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月加入哈国国籍；但<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其被强行驾车驶入中国霍尔果斯口岸至哈国国际市场路段的哈国境内自由贸易区的中国新疆警方跨境绑架，自此失联；尽管其已移民并加入哈国国籍，但仍被中共政府视为新疆居民，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被伊犁哈萨克自治州霍城县警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被霍城县警方以同罪由转正式逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其案被霍城县检察院以“间谍罪”和“诈骗罪”起诉至新疆维吾尔自治区高级法院伊犁哈萨克自治州分院，指控其曾在伊犁州政府移民管理局任职期间，结识了哈国民族安全委员会成员，并按其要求对伊犁河流域水利设施及河流进行拍照，提供水利设施信息等，该行为触犯了中国法律，属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其被该法院秘密审判，以“间谍罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，以“诈骗罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，数罪并罚，最后执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。目前被羁押于伊犁哈萨克自治州霍城县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿提开姆•茹孜：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1991</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐市人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Atikem Rozi</span>，又译为阿提克木·如孜，维吾尔著名学者伊力哈木•土赫提的学生<span lang="EN-US">,</span>“维吾尔在线”网站前义工，维吾尔人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2010</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年—<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，曾因个人护照申请连续三次被当局以政治原因而拒发（尽管其无任何政治不良记录），故而将其遭遇发布于新浪微博之上，随后各大媒体，如官方刊物《都市北京》<span lang="EN-US">(Metro Beijing)</span>、“维吾尔在线”和中国《环球时报》等媒体便竞相刊发或转载了涉及其本人与其他维吾尔人申请护照时遭遇双重标准的文章，引发社会热议；此一事件因很快触动了中共当局的敏感神经，遂遭到中共新疆当局的严厉打击和报复；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，被乌鲁木齐警方以在“媒体上辩论”为由传唤，且被审问<span lang="EN-US">6</span>小时后才得以获释，两天之后又到其家继续威吓、骚扰；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因其多次使用<span lang="EN-US">twitter,facebook</span>以及新浪微博等网站发布文章和讯息，并利用网媒广泛寻找被失踪多日的男友、维吾尔人权捍卫者穆塔力普•伊明，随被以背景是维吾尔著名学者伊力哈木•土赫提在北京的学生、曾是“维吾尔在线”网站义工为罪由被北京市警方传唤，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日其等<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人被以涉嫌“分裂国家罪” 统一刑拘（但据官方报道，其于<span lang="EN-US">2014 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">1 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被拘留）；同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因其案被定为“分裂国家犯罪集团案”，故被新疆乌鲁木齐市检察院正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月后，其一行<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人案在乌鲁木齐巿中级法院一起开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人终被乌鲁木齐巿中级法院统一宣判<span lang="EN-US">3-8</span>年不等刑期；其中，其被以“分裂主义罪”和“危害国家安全罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，理应刑满释放，但据中国环球电视网（又称中国国际电视台，英文简称<span lang="EN-US">CGTN</span>）在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月发布的一部宣传片中显示，其身着囚服出现在镜头前，故其是否如期释放，或是否被释放后又重新拘留，不得而知。目前或仍在新疆女子监狱（又名新疆第二监狱，新疆乌鲁木齐市新市区东站路<span lang="EN-US">1327</span>号女子监狱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">830013</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_5.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_5.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿旺觉尼（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">出生年月不详，籍贯不详（只知藏区僧人），西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺密宗学院经师，学者僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自幼成为僧侣，并长期在西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺密宗学院研习、进修；因曾长期师从藏族著名佛学教师兰林仁波切（<span lang="EN-US">Lamrim<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Rinpoche</span>），成为其主要弟子之一，遂被哲蚌寺密宗学院立为经师（即精通佛教经藏的僧人，又称佛教讲经诵经的师父）；又由于其受教尊师兰林仁波切是深受藏民普遍敬重的哲蚌寺喇嘛，地位、声望及影响力并非由政府任命，因此被当局视为异己予以排挤、管控，其因与之交往甚密，故而亦成为当局长期监控打压的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因藏区发生以僧侣为主的大规模抗议示威活动，以期达到让中共当局真正实现（或兑现）藏民族“自治独立”，并呼吁准许达赖喇嘛回国返乡等政治诉求，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其所在哲蚌寺<span lang="EN-US">350</span>名僧侣亦参与其中，致使抗议行动很快扩展至整个拉萨市区及四川、青海等藏区；针对此，西藏当局很快派遣大批持枪武警予以极端管控，双方发生严重对峙与冲突，随后即有众多僧侣被抓捕，其余人等被遣返寺庙严加看守；尽管此前其并未参与游行抗议，但是，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日其仍被拉萨市警方以涉嫌“参与抗议活动”抓捕，自此长期失联；另有二名哲蚌寺好友、学者僧侣亦被一同抓捕；后被拉萨市检察院转正式批捕，罪由竟是“未能阻止哲蚌寺僧人举行大规模抗议行动”；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，在被长期羁押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久后，被拉萨市中级法院以不详罪名密判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，因长期失联，其狱中具体境况均无下落。目前疑似在拉萨曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿旺益西：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">藏族，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年代出生，西藏自治区拉萨市林周县人，拉萨市林周县旁多乡村民，生态环境保护者，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。自</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1998</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年始，中共西藏当局即在西藏拉萨所辖的林周县旁多乡境内对各种矿产资源进行初步勘探，并为防止当地藏人进行抗议，曾特意宣布将为无业藏人提供工作机会等，但在正式开工采矿，且顺利修建“旁多水利枢纽工程”之后，当局不仅不兑现之前的承诺，反而随意开采矿区，使得当地生态环境遭受严重破坏（如）；迫于无耐，当地藏人遂多次向相关部门提出反映与投诉；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2009</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月，西藏当局为确保水利工程及采矿等计划顺利实行，开始强令旁多乡</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">119</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">户（近</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">700</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">名）村民集体搬迁；因当地藏民拒不搬迁，虽数次向主管部门提出投诉请求，均毫无果效，随于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2011</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被迫开展和平示威活动，试图阻拦破坏生态环境的采矿项目，但又遭到中共军警的残酷镇压；很快，阿旺益西与另</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">名村民维权代表均被拉萨市警方野蛮抓捕，自此失联；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2012</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，在被超期拘押长达</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年多之久后，其一行</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">人“请愿游行案”在拉萨市中级法院开庭受理，均被以“试图分裂西藏，并组织领导了以保护环境为名的抗议活动”罪由分别重判</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8-12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年不等刑期，其中，阿旺益西被秘密判处有期徒刑</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，刑期至</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月。目前在西藏自治区第一监狱（原拉萨市扎其监狱）服刑。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿吾勒别克·努尔加合蒲（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1978</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，哈萨克族名<span lang="EN-US">Ayelbek Nurzhahp</span>，伊犁州昭苏县阿克达拉镇清真寺伊玛目（即宗教仪式领祷人或主持），中国在押良心犯。早年曾就读于伊犁特克斯县宗教学校，毕业后被官方指定为昭苏县清真寺的伊玛目（即宗教仪式领祷人或主持），管辖服务于当地<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个清真寺；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾多次到哈萨克共和国（简称哈国）访问；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因感觉新疆政治气氛欠佳而将妻子和两个孩子送到哈国，其本人亦打算将自己在新疆的不动产（包括牲畜等）变卖后移民哈国，不料被中共新疆当局知晓，遂被警方以“不准移民哈国”为由抓捕，并遭威胁让其全家（含其妻子和孩子）务必返回国内生活；其全家虽按要求照办，但<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日仍被昭苏县警方突然抓走，并被关押在当地的政治再教育营；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被昭苏县警方以“全家要移民哈国”为罪由正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，知其被伊犁哈萨克自治州昭苏县法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">25</span>年，罪名不详，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2042</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日；据悉，在被判决时，法院竟称让其“自己选择罪名，然后给判刑”；其妻、其弟被送政治再教育营教育，后亦被以同罪由各判<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年。目前在生产建设兵团农七师高泉监狱（新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">833200</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿亚桑扎（藏族）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">青海省果洛州牧民。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿亚桑扎是因为上访被抓捕的，<span lang="EN-US"> 2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，因为他经牧民选举当上牧委会主任，却被官方把<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年已经了结的案件，重新拿出来说事把他抓捕冤屈判刑一年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，上诉也被维持原判。阿亚桑扎<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午在果洛州高速路口上访途中，被公安人员抓捕连夜送到西宁次日送到了乐都区看守所。阿亚桑扎对自己被关押到离果洛州<span lang="EN-US">600</span>公里外的看守所感到不可理解，认为这是官方对他的一种折磨。他被抓时正在带领大家控告相关人员贪污犯罪的事情进展情况，要大家继续坚持控告下去。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，阿亚桑扎被当局判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑。阿亚桑扎等所谓涉恶案件开庭两天当庭宣判，其对获刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年当庭表示不服提起上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">艾朝玉<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">成都市法轮功学员。刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被成都公安局成华分局国保、双水碾派出所警察抄家并抓捕。刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被成华区公安分局批捕，关押在郫县看守所。构陷他们的所谓「案件」曾两次退回侦查机关。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，成华区检察院把刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇起诉到成华区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午，刘伟、艾朝玉夫妇，在成都市成华区法院一楼视频开庭，分别被判刑八年。庭审结束后，夫妻俩与家人坚决不服判决，马上要求上诉，并请律师继续代理二审。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">艾则孜•艾买提（维吾尔）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">47</span>岁，新疆阿克苏地区维族教长。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月因皮山县一个村市集从事宗教教学活动，被当地公安局拘捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被判入狱<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安然：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">本名崔浩新、济南回民作家、诗人（即推友<span lang="EN-US">@ismaelan </span>）。安然现年<span lang="EN-US">41</span>岁的安然曾在官方刊物发表过自己的作品，其中有作品被收录到中国作家协会编选的“新时期少数民族文学选”。他早前发表的《我的诗歌志》，记录其诗歌生涯中有一大部分为关注新疆的内容。此前<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月曾因在推特转发和发布的有关新疆“再教育营”的报道和文字等言论遭警方抓捕，后都有惊无险获释。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日即农历春节除夕夜遭济南警方刑事拘留，罪名是寻衅滋事。目前音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安彦魁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">基督徒，山西郇城归正教会传道。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，安彦魁传道和张乘豪被山西汾阳的吕梁县公安局带走，似与此前汾阳五位基督教徒被以“偷越边境罪”刑拘、逮捕一案有关。安彦魁、张乘豪和汾阳五位基督教徒都曾在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月底，到马来西亚亚吉隆坡参加唐崇荣牧师组织的“<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>福音与文化大会”。当时他们都是持护照从海关正常出入，并无违法行为。后教会五位弟兄于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午被刑事拘留，被抓捕的理由竟然是“偷越边境”。后安彦魁传道于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被汾阳市公安局以涉嫌偷越国境罪刑事拘留，现羁押在孝义市看守所。安彦魁传道被刑事拘留后，其妻子姚聪娅表示：“<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年初，安彦魁拿着中华人民共和国给办理的护照，和合法签证手续去了马来西亚，连走带回顶多一周的时间。发这个信息为的是大家为我们家能有更多祷告，也是安慰为我们挂心的亲人。更想警戎周围的亲人朋友们出国游玩要警慎，免得哪天也被定个什么偷越罪……”<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_59.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_59.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">昂扎（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区比如县人，原比如镇孟庆村干部，政治异议人士，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年以来，一直担任那曲地区比如镇孟庆村的村干部；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，因中共当局在其所在县各乡村展开‘爱国再教育运动’，并强迫藏民在各家屋顶上悬挂五星红旗，此举引起比如县农牧民、学生、僧人、尼姑、作家、歌手等各类人士的同声抗议，并发起连串示威活动，成为继<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年后在西藏自治区内最大的示威抗议活动，随引发中共当局的极度恐惧，将比如县视为极不稳定地区，曾先后集结大批军警实施“维稳”，肆意拘捕僧俗藏人，对当地有影响力的藏人处以重刑，并采取‘对内严厉打击示威民众，对外严密封锁消息’等严打措施；在此背景下，昂扎所在孟庆村的藏民亦因参与了公开抗议与示威活动，遂遭致当局的严酷打压，于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被当地警方以涉嫌“参与抗议示威”，“秘密组织相关人员在家里召开会议”等罪由刑拘，后被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被当地法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罪名不详。目前在西藏自治区一家监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">奥坎（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生不详，新疆维吾尔自治区阿尔泰地区人，哈萨克族，穆斯林，伊犁哈萨克自治州阿尔泰地区哈巴河县清真寺阿訇（即伊斯兰宗教事务主持人），伊斯兰知名宗教领袖，中国在押良心犯。近年来，因新疆地区局势日益紧张，中共当局加强了对新疆各民族在宗教信仰上的高压管控手段和措施，哈萨克族人也不例外；这期间，因奥坎是阿尔泰地区哈萨克族群中知名宗教界领袖，影响力大，遂当局严密监控，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年又因其按照本民族及宗教习俗为死者做了传统的祷告仪式，被当地警方偷拍，随后即以此问罪，被抓刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初，其被阿尔泰地区哈巴河县法院以不具名罪名秘判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前羁押或服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">B. <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">巴依木拉提·那如孜别克（哈）、巴和提古丽·吾力拜依（哈）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">巴给拉·吾力拜依（哈）、巴鲁宁、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">白宝华、白国显、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">白海英、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">白玉福、白玉珍、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">白玛益西（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">班阔吉（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">边巴杰布（藏）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">边雪梅、边彦娟、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">别丽花、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">包国华、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">包万明</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">鲍乃刚、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卞丽潮、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">别热克汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>朵兰汗（哈萨克）、别依力汗•萨合达提及其儿子（哈萨克）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、不列斯白克•叶尔买克巴依（哈）、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">巴依木拉提·那如孜别克（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1990</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，哈萨克族，伊宁县卡拉亚尕奇乡奥依曼布拉克村居民，职业不详，哈萨克斯坦国绿卡持有者，中国在押政治犯。巴依木拉提·那如孜别克早期曾到上海市某高中上学；毕业后，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月又曾前往中国邻国——哈萨克共和国（又称哈萨克斯坦国，简称“哈国”），在阿拉木图市大学攻读学位，并于同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月返回中国新疆；因其在哈国留学期间曾获取绿卡（即拥有哈国永久居住权），回国生活数载后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，突然被新疆伊宁县警方莫名抓走，送当地政治教育中心接受“再教育培训”（实则被监禁羁押）；被囚长达<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月后，因其对培训方式及内容等心存抵触，培训结果表现不佳，故不仅未被释放返家，反被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，被新疆伊宁县法院一审以不明罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。目前被羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">巴和提古丽·吾力拜依：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1977</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市人，哈萨克族名<span lang="EN-US"> Baktgul Oralbaikizi</span>，穆斯林信徒，前伊犁哈萨克自治州《奎屯日报》记者，中国在押良心犯。 早年曾一直在新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯日报社任职当记者，后与其兄长及小妹先后前往哈萨克斯坦国创业；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2016</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，原西藏自治区党委书记陈全国调任新疆当一把手，因强化要加强对新疆地区的管控，要求工作及生活在海外的维吾尔族、哈萨克族等中国公民（含海外留学生）必须立刻返回中国生活，其随与众哈萨克族同胞纷纷返回新疆； 回国后最初两年，除去其护照被地方当局没收、出国权利受限外，生活尚能平安顺利，直至<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其突遭伊犁州奎屯市警方莫名抓捕，并送一家政治再教育转化营羁押，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其家人从奎屯市警方处得知，其被伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，罪名不清，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2037</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月；据悉，其丈夫受牵连屡遭警方恐吓威胁，被要求与妻子尽早离婚，被其断然拒绝。 目前在新疆新源监狱（新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州新源县，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">868813</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">巴给拉·吾力拜依：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，哈萨克族，<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市人，哈萨克族名<span lang="EN-US">Bagila Oralbaikizi</span>，穆斯林信徒，个体商户经营者、理发店老板，奎屯市公民，中国在押良心犯。曾在伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市经营一家理发店十余年，后与兄长及姐姐先后前往哈萨克斯坦国创业；<span lang="EN-US"> 2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，因原西藏自治区党委书记陈全国调任新疆当一把手，强化要加强对新疆地区的控制，遂要求凡去海外留学、工作及生活的维吾尔族、哈萨克族等中国公民必须尽快返回国内生活，故其随与其兄姊及众哈萨克族同胞纷纷返回新疆；回国之初，政府当局虽将其护照予以没收、出国权利受到限制，但日常生活尚属平安顺利，直至<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其及其兄姊均遭伊犁州奎屯市警方突然抓捕，并送当地某政治再教育转化营关押，自此失去联系；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其家人从奎屯市警方处获悉，其被伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，罪名不清，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2033</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月；据悉，其丈夫屡遭警方施压，被要求与其妻离婚，被其夫断然拒绝。目前在新疆生产建设兵团农七师奎屯监狱（新疆维吾尔自治区<span lang="EN-US">/</span>克拉玛依市<span lang="EN-US">/</span>克拉玛依区<span lang="EN-US">/</span>共青镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">834034</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">巴鲁宁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">网名“迦南”，山东烟台公民。出生在一个飞行世家，早年接受过民主启蒙，一直活跃在互联网上，微信号被封号<span lang="EN-US">7-8</span>次。最近支持香港反送中期间，巴鲁宁在各微信群中发表言论声援香港。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日早<span lang="EN-US">5:00</span>被烟台市公安局福山分局国保支队抓捕后关押并刑事拘留。目前羁押在烟台市看守所。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">白宝华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">内蒙古赤峰市元宝山区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">56</span>岁左右，农村妇女，没有收入，家庭以收破烂维持生活。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午十一点左右，赤峰市元宝山区元宝山镇派出所韩立民带领三个便衣去白宝华家骚扰，非法抄家，抢劫大法书籍、台历（<span lang="EN-US">500</span>本左右）、<span lang="EN-US">14000</span>元现金及很多个人物品，并把白宝华抓捕。其中这<span lang="EN-US">14000</span>元是白宝华用来给儿子治大腿血栓从亲戚朋友处借来的钱，都被抢去说成是用来做法轮功资料。随后，白宝华被送至元宝山区看守所关押。后白宝华被赤峰中级法院宣判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">白国显：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。白国显被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">白海英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南昆明市法轮功学员。白海英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日在昆明市盘龙区白龙路德胜家居世博店上班刚吃完饭时被盘龙公安分局小坝派出所警察强行搜查随身物品，在包中发现<span lang="EN-US">8</span>本法轮功宣传册，随后抄家抢走<span lang="EN-US">109</span>本书籍和<span lang="EN-US">167</span>本小册子等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被盘龙公安局逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，盘公安分局向西山检察院提交了起诉意见书。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日上午，白海英被西山法院第<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次视频开庭；判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">白玉福：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江大庆市被迫流离失所的法轮功学员。原大庆市石油管理局测井公司武保科科长；妻子张立新，原大庆石油管理局物业二公司乘风热力分公司职工。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，白玉福和张立新开始修炼法轮功，按真、善、忍标准做好人。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，白玉福、张立新夫妇多次被中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，白玉福、张立新夫妇在辽宁省阜新市彰武县被警方抓捕，后刑事拘留、批捕、起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被彰武县法院视频开庭。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日获悉，白玉福被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，张立新被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。白玉福刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">白玉珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">河南省信阳市浉河区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1911</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日法轮功学员白玉珍、靳玉玲被信阳市警察入室抓捕，后被构陷至信阳市潢川县检察院、法院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在看守所遭开庭。靳玉玲<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁；白玉珍老人<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁，进法庭时，身体走路都不稳。在开庭过程中，靳玉玲、白玉珍一直还被强制戴着手铐。靳玉玲被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；白玉珍被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。白玉珍刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/2022-1-20.html#zip4</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">白玛益西（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年出生，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Pema Yeshi</span>，四川省甘孜藏族自治州新龙县人，甘孜藏族自治州新龙县塘吉乡（音译）尼达村农民，藏族人权捍卫者。曾因积极参与罢耕运动和抵制中共控制的藏历新年庆祝活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被当局怀疑参与在该县塘吉乡（音译）境内的一起有关抗议中共暴政，散发传单、呼吁西藏独立的示威活动；事发当天因该抗议活动引发警民冲突，乡政府办公大楼发生火灾，<span lang="EN-US"> 2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，随于被新龙县警方强行抓捕，并被以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”和“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留，关押于四川省成都市某看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被四川省甘孜州中级法院以“煽动分裂国家”和“扰乱社会秩序”两项罪名判处死刑，缓期两年执行，后改判为无期徒刑。目前在四川省德阳市黄许镇德阳监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">班阔吉（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，女，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县城关镇人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者、政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾在当地发生示威活动时，因政治诉求而两次遭到当局数月拘押，获释后一直处于被严密监控中。<span lang="EN-US"> 2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日突然再次被抓，自此失联，后得知她被指控涉嫌“组织阿坝民众举办达赖喇嘛尊者八十岁寿辰活动”而遭逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，据悉当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">边巴杰布</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：藏族，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年代出生，又称边巴坚参，西藏自治区拉萨市林周县人，拉萨市林周县旁多乡村民，职业不详，生态环境保护者，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。自</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1998</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年始，中共西藏当局即在西藏拉萨所辖的林周县旁多乡境内对各种矿产资源进行初步勘探，并为防止当地藏人进行抗议，曾特意宣布将为无业藏人提供工作机会等，但在正式开工采矿，且顺利修建“旁多水利枢纽工程”之后，当局不仅不兑现之前的承诺，反而随意开采矿区，使得当地生态环境遭受严重破坏；迫于无耐，当地藏人遂多次向相关部门提出反映与投诉，但毫无效果； </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2009</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月，西藏当局为确保水利工程及采矿等计划如期举行，开始强令旁多乡</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">119</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">户（近</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">700</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">名）村民集体搬迁；后因当地藏民拒绝搬迁，数次向主管部门提出长久居住要求，均无果效，随于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2011</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月，被迫开展和平抗议活动，以期借此拦阻当局破坏生态环境的采矿项目，但又遭到中共军警的残酷镇压； 很快，边巴杰布及另</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">名维权村民代表被拉萨市警方野蛮抓捕，自此失联；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2012</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，边巴杰布家属获悉，在被秘押长达一年多之久后，其一行</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">人“请愿游行案”在拉萨市中级法院开庭受理，均被以“试图分裂西藏，并组织领导了以保护环境为名的抗议活动”罪由重判</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8-12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年不等刑期，其中，边巴杰布与另两名维权藏人（曲嘉唯色、阿旺益西）分别被秘密判处有期徒刑</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，刑期至</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月。目前在西藏自治区第一监狱（原拉萨市扎其监狱）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">边雪梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省衡阳市衡山县法轮功学员。家住湖南省衡阳市衡山县开云镇。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，边雪梅被衡山长江派出所颜永初恶意举报，遭一伙警察闯入家中绑架。警察抢走她家中所有修炼用的经书、其它各种私人物品以及四千多元人民币。边雪梅被关押到衡阳市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午，衡山县检察院、法院对边雪梅非法开庭，当庭没有结果。据悉，法官要边雪梅当庭认罪保证今后不再炼法轮功，否则要判刑。边雪梅，一直讲真相，表示，按真善忍做好人没有错。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，衡山县法院再次对边雪梅视频开庭，宣称对边雪梅判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，所谓理由不是法律条文，而是法轮功学员边雪梅“拒不认错”，“不配合”。此后，被非法关押在衡阳市第一看守所的边雪梅仍被看守所和法院人员逼写“保证书”。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">边彦娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北辛集法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，河北省辛集市南智邱镇南棚村李月棉和辛集市马庄乡北营村郑艳梅、边彦娟因讲法轮功真相被大屯派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日第二次开庭，律师又充分的做了无罪辩护，法官说结果要等通知，然后因为疫情一直到三月份律师才得知结果，三人都被判刑，刑期分别为：李月棉<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元；郑艳梅<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">9</span>千元；边彦娟<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。后得知，这三名法轮功学员已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日都被关押到石家庄女子监狱服刑。边彦娟刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">别丽花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省双辽市法轮功学员。别丽花女士在双辽发电厂工作，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被双辽国保大队长伙同双辽公安局辽西派出所警察从工作单位抓捕，并对她住所搜查。别丽花先被关押在双辽看守所，后来又转到四平市看守所。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">包国华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">浙江金华圣爱堂牧师，于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被金华市公安局婺城分局以涉嫌非法经营罪、聚众扰乱社会秩序罪、隐匿会计凭证罪、侵占罪四个罪名刑事拘留。被抓之前，包牧师曾拒绝金华市宗教局强制整改（实质是拆除）新教堂顶部的十字架。包国华牧师拒绝的理由是<span lang="EN-US">-----</span>新教堂的施工、规划手续齐全，不是违法建筑，不应当整改（拆除）。在被拘留后的第<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日金华日报、浙江卫视以“清廉牧师”的贪婪人生大篇幅报道包国华牧师及其妻子邢文香牧师的所谓犯罪事实。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，包国华牧师被金华市婺城区法院控告犯有“职务侵占罪”、“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”、“非法经营罪”以及“隐匿会计凭证、会计账簿、财务会计报告罪”等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>项罪名，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，并处没收财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">60</span>万元，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">包万明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江鸡西市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>出生。鸡西市法轮功学员周克铭在发放法轮功资料时，被人诬告。鸡西市公安局鸡冠区公安分局国保、永昌派出所、铁西派出所采取跟踪、监控手段，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日抓捕了包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭被非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被非法关押在鸡西市看守所<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。包万明、周克铭、滕淑丽，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日遭鸡东法院以视频的方式开庭，近日得知，包万明被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、罚金十万元；滕淑丽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>万元；周克铭被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。包万明刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">鲍乃刚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北京山维权人士。男，湖北省京山县宋河镇人，复转军官，曾在绵阳市北川县经商，因为父上访申冤<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，被当局栽赃入监两年。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，因在网上响应茉莉花革命，被当局以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，后羁押于绵阳市看守所长达<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，之后被逮捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被取保获释送回原籍湖北。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，鲍乃刚因旁听武汉王芳涉嫌寻衅滋事案庭审遭户籍地京山县公安局行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日处罚。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，鲍乃刚向京山县人民法院对京山县公安局提起行政诉状，要求撤销京山县公安局京公（宋河）行决字<span lang="EN-US">1101</span>号行政处罚决定书，责令恶意剥夺公民权利的京山县公安局向公众公开道歉。后遭法院枉法判决。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日鲍乃刚刚到北京就被湖北京山维稳人员强行劫持，押解回当地，第二天，鲍乃刚在京山公安局接受询问并被抄家，警方拿走了鲍乃刚的电脑、手机，以及一些上诉材料等。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日鲍乃刚被京山警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。案件在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日开庭审理，开庭至今未有宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日鲍乃刚的辩护律师吴魁明收到经办法官的电话通知，法庭当日在湖北京山市看守所宣判鲍乃刚涉嫌寻衅滋事罪一案，鲍乃刚被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。鲍乃刚表示要上诉。二审维持原判。现关押在京山市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">卞丽潮：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1966</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，河北省人，原河北省唐山市开滦第十中学教师，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。曾因信仰和修炼法轮功，而遭到中共警方长期监控；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年初，因中共当局通过监控手段得知有法轮功学员从事光盘盒生意，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，统一部署，以“大案”“要案”为目标，在河北、辽宁、山东等十数个省份集结各地国保、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”派出所警员，按照监听查获的名单，野蛮逮捕了一百多名法轮功学员，卞丽潮亦因法轮功学员身份而被河北省唐山市警方刑拘；逮捕刑拘期间，多次遭遇严刑逼供，其妻女受到严厉威胁，其家被抄，且家中做生意用的流动资金（注：其被抓走时，家中约有十几万元现金，尚未来得及存入银行）竟被警方非法侵占，并以开假单据方式诱骗其妻签字，谎称是法轮功资金，以示为“证据”；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被河北省唐山市中级法院以“信仰、修炼法轮功邪教”为罪由重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。最初在河北省保定监狱服刑，因其不堪忍受狱中酷刑折磨（注：狱方每天会派<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个狱警带着<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个犯人对其进行轮番“包夹”监控、折磨），致其心脏病等病情严重恶化，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日起转到河北省石家庄第四监狱第八监区服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">别热克汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>朵兰汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州塔城地区额敏县人，塔城地区额敏县某清真寺主持，官派任命阿訇，良心犯。曾在清真寺主持工作<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，但仍因宗教信仰自由问题而被塔城地区额敏县警方于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年上半年拘捕，后被当局指控为：未经许可，以伊斯兰教传统方式给一对哈萨克族新婚人念尼卡，而这对婚夫妇在婚礼的第二天才正式登记领取结婚证，此举触犯了中共“其极端化”法令，于是很快被宣布逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被伊犁哈萨克自治州塔城地区法院以“从事非法宗教活动罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年。目前具体服刑地点不详，只知他被羁押在新疆昌吉州一所用来囚禁政治犯的大监狱中。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">别依力汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>萨合达提及其儿子：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆阿尔泰地区青河县阿热勒乡清真寺阿訇别依力汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>萨合达提，男，哈萨克族，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年春天被抓，至今无下落，。别依力汗的儿子，因在哈国官方宗教学校学过三个月的宗教知识，也被公安带走羁押。而别依力汗<span lang="EN-US">.</span>萨合达提家族，在青河县属著名的宗教家族，他的父亲、爷爷都是阿訇，在当地有极高的知名度。由于百姓对其家族的尊敬，引来当局的恐惧，故遭迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">不列斯白克•叶尔买克巴依（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，新疆伊犁霍城县人，伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州霍城县生产建设兵团小麻扎<span lang="EN-US">61</span>团光明路<span lang="EN-US">084</span>号公民，哈萨克族，穆斯林，中国在押良心犯。被捕前，曾与家人海外旅游并暂留哈萨克斯坦共和国居住；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年返回中国后，不久即被伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州霍城县警方没收护照；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年前后，被以不明罪由（疑指对中共当局思想不忠等）抓捕，送入霍城县“教育培训中心”（又称“再教育营”）接受中共洗脑式教育，自此失联；后因在该“培训中心”拒绝认罪和配合接受再教育方式及其要求，遂被霍城县警方正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，被新疆伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州霍城县法院一审以不确罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年初。目前疑似在新疆伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州新源监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
</div>
